> message("  NA в condition: ", n_na_cond)
NA в condition: 28
> message("  NA в genotype:  ", n_na_geno)
NA в genotype:  0
> message("  Уникальных образцов: ", n_samples)
Уникальных образцов: 14
> print(table(all_scores\$condition, useNA = "always"))

          WT     PPM1A_KO     PPM1B_KO    Double_KO       WT_TNF PPM1A_KO_TNF PPM1B_KO_TNF         <NA> 
          42           42           42            0           14           14           14           28 
    > stopifnot(

+ "NA в condition после join" = n_na_cond == 0,
+ "NA в genotype после join"  = n_na_geno == 0,
+ "Не все 14 образцов"        = n_samples == 14
+ )
Error: NA в condition после join

Всё ясно — Double KO в coldata называется `"DKO_basal"`, не `"Double_KO_basal"`. Исправляем только маппинг:

```r
group_to_condition <- c(
  "WT_basal"          = "WT",
  "PPM1D_KO_basal"    = "PPM1D_KO",
  "PPM1B_KO_basal"    = "PPM1B_KO",
  "DKO_basal"         = "DKO",          # <-- было Double_KO_basal
  "WT_TNF12h"         = "WT_TNF",
  "PPM1D_KO_TNF12h"   = "PPM1D_KO_TNF",
  "PPM1B_KO_TNF12h"   = "PPM1B_KO_TNF"
)

condition_levels <- c(
  "WT", "PPM1D_KO", "PPM1B_KO", "DKO",
  "WT_TNF", "PPM1D_KO_TNF", "PPM1B_KO_TNF"
)

# Палитры под реальные имена
condition_colors <- c(
  "WT"            = "#4DAF4A",
  "PPM1D_KO"      = "#E41A1C",
  "PPM1B_KO"      = "#FF7F00",
  "DKO"           = "#984EA3",
  "WT_TNF"        = "#A6D96A",
  "PPM1D_KO_TNF"  = "#FB9A99",
  "PPM1B_KO_TNF"  = "#FDBF6F"
)

genotype_colors <- c(
  "WT"       = "#4DAF4A",
  "PPM1D_KO" = "#E41A1C",
  "PPM1B_KO" = "#FF7F00",
  "DKO"      = "#984EA3"
)
```

Затем пересчитай `all_scores` с тем же join-кодом что уже работал:

```r
all_scores <- all_scores_raw %>%
  left_join(
    coldata %>%
      select(any_of(c("sample", "sample_id",
                      "genotype", "tnf",
                      "group", "n_replicates", "exploratory"))),
    by = setNames(
      intersect(c("sample", "sample_id"), names(coldata)),
      "sample"
    )
  ) %>%
  mutate(
    condition = factor(
      recode(as.character(group), !!!group_to_condition),
      levels = condition_levels
    )
  )

# Проверка
message("NA в condition: ", sum(is.na(all_scores$condition)))
print(table(all_scores$condition, useNA = "always"))
```

**Итого реальные имена в coldata:**


| Что ожидали | Что реально в coldata |
| :-- | :-- |
| `Double_KO_basal` | `DKO_basal` |
| `Double_KO` (genotype) | `DKO` |
| `PPM1A_KO` | `PPM1D_KO` |

Больше никаких `PPM1A_KO` — используем `PPM1D_KO` везде, это биологически правильное название (PPM1D = Wip1, а не PPM1A).

---

# > message("\n── score_matrix: ", nrow(score_matrix), " × ", ncol(score_matrix))

── score_matrix: 14 × 7
> \# =============================================================================
> \# 12. Fig_SEN_01: Heatmap средних скоров по группам
> \# =============================================================================
> col_fun <- colorRamp2(

+ c(-1.5, -0.75, 0, 0.75, 1.5),
+ c("\#2166AC", "\#92C5DE", "white", "\#F4A582", "\#B2182B")
+ )
> \# Аннотация столбцов
> col_vec <- condition_colors[colnames(score_matrix)]
> col_ann <- HeatmapAnnotation(
+ Condition = colnames(score_matrix),
+ col       = list(Condition = col_vec),
+ show_legend          = TRUE,
+ annotation_name_side = "left",
+ annotation_name_gp   = gpar(fontsize = 9)
+ )
Error: elements in `col` should be named vectors.

Причина ошибки: `HeatmapAnnotation` требует чтобы в `col` вектор был именован **значениями аннотации**, а не просто цветами. Вот исправленный блок секции 12:

```r
# =============================================================================
# 12. Fig_SEN_01: Heatmap средних скоров по группам
# =============================================================================
col_fun <- colorRamp2(
  c(-1.5, -0.75, 0, 0.75, 1.5),
  c("#2166AC", "#92C5DE", "white", "#F4A582", "#B2182B")
)

# Реальные имена условий в матрице (после всех исправлений)
cond_in_matrix <- colnames(score_matrix)

# Именованный вектор цветов — имена ДОЛЖНЫ совпадать со значениями аннотации
col_vec <- condition_colors[cond_in_matrix]
names(col_vec) <- cond_in_matrix   # <-- ЭТО БЫЛО ПОТЕРЯНО

# Аннотация столбцов — передаём вектор значений, col = список с именованным вектором
col_ann <- HeatmapAnnotation(
  Condition = cond_in_matrix,                      # вектор значений
  col       = list(Condition = col_vec),           # именованный вектор цветов
  show_legend          = TRUE,
  annotation_name_side = "left",
  annotation_name_gp   = gpar(fontsize = 9)
)

# Аннотация строк
module_map <- c(
  "sen_core"         = "Senescence Core",
  "sen_ois"          = "Senescence Core",
  "Senescence_DDR"   = "Senescence Core",
  "Senescence_SASP"  = "SASP / Inflammation",
  "sen_sasp"         = "SASP / Inflammation",
  "Inflammaging"     = "SASP / Inflammation",
  "sen_ddr"          = "DDR",
  "cGAS_STING"       = "DDR",
  "sen_mitochondria" = "Mito / Stress",
  "Mito_Stress"      = "Mito / Stress",
  "Rho_Activity"     = "Cytoskeleton",
  "ProxTubule"       = "Kidney",
  "Tyshkovskiy_DNAmAge"       = "Aging Clocks",
  "Tyshkovskiy_LongevityUp"   = "Aging Clocks",
  "Tyshkovskiy_LongevityDown" = "Aging Clocks",
  "Aging_DNAmAge"    = "Aging Clocks",
  "Aging_LongevityUp"   = "Aging Clocks",
  "Aging_LongevityDown" = "Aging Clocks"
)

module_colors <- c(
  "Senescence Core"     = "#D9534F",
  "SASP / Inflammation" = "#F0AD4E",
  "DDR"                 = "#5B9BD5",
  "Mito / Stress"       = "#70AD47",
  "Cytoskeleton"        = "#9B59B6",
  "Kidney"              = "#1ABC9C",
  "Aging Clocks"        = "#95A5A6",
  "Other"               = "#CCCCCC"
)

row_modules <- module_map[rownames(score_matrix)]
row_modules[is.na(row_modules)] <- "Other"

# Именованный вектор для rowAnnotation — имена = значения аннотации
used_modules      <- unique(row_modules)
row_module_colors <- module_colors[used_modules]
names(row_module_colors) <- used_modules   # <-- то же самое правило

row_ann <- rowAnnotation(
  Module = row_modules,
  col    = list(Module = row_module_colors),
  show_legend          = TRUE,
  annotation_name_side = "top",
  annotation_name_gp   = gpar(fontsize = 9)
)

png("output/figures/senescence/Fig_SEN_01_heatmap_group_means.png",
    width = 2600, height = 2000, res = 200)

ht <- Heatmap(
  score_matrix,
  name             = "Mean\nZ-score",
  col              = col_fun,
  top_annotation   = col_ann,
  right_annotation = row_ann,
  cluster_rows     = FALSE,
  cluster_columns  = FALSE,
  row_names_side   = "left",
  row_names_gp     = gpar(fontsize = 10),
  column_names_gp  = gpar(fontsize = 10),
  column_names_rot = 35,
  rect_gp          = gpar(col = "white", lwd = 0.8),
  cell_fun = function(j, i, x, y, width, height, fill) {
    grid.text(
      sprintf("%.2f", score_matrix[i, j]),
      x, y,
      gp = gpar(
        fontsize = 8,
        col = ifelse(abs(score_matrix[i, j]) > 0.8, "white", "black")
      )
    )
  },
  heatmap_legend_param = list(
    direction = "vertical",
    title_gp  = gpar(fontsize = 9, fontface = "bold"),
    labels_gp = gpar(fontsize = 8)
  )
)

draw(ht, padding = unit(c(5, 15, 5, 5), "mm"))
dev.off()
message("✓ Fig_SEN_01 сохранён")
```

**Суть бага:** `condition_colors[cond_in_matrix]` возвращает вектор с именами из `condition_colors` (т.е. теми же ключами), но `HeatmapAnnotation` сверяет имена вектора со значениями переданной аннотации — они должны совпадать **один-в-один**. Строка `names(col_vec) <- cond_in_matrix` это гарантирует.

---

# пиши скрипт 04 в окне чата, я сам его запушу в репо, старый скрипт был такой:

# 04_module_clocks_v2.R

# 

# БИОЛОГИЧЕСКИЙ СМЫСЛ:

# "Module clocks" — это многомерные биологические часы:

# несколько скоров (DDR, Inflammaging, Rho, ProxTubule, SASP)

# визуализируются как спицы радарной диаграммы ("clockface").

# Это позволяет увидеть ПРОФИЛЬ состояния клетки, а не отдельные метрики.

# 

# НОВЫЕ АСПЕКТЫ:

# 

# 1. DOUBLE KO — позиционирование на радаре:

# Если Double_KO занимает позицию "дальше от центра", чем оба

# Single KOs по всем осям → синергия.

# Если по одним осям = WipKO, по другим = Ppm1b_KO → независимые роли.

# 

# 2. TNF-ТРАЕКТОРИЯ:

# Наносим вектор "ctrl → TNF" для каждого генотипа.

# Длина вектора = величина сдвига при TNF-стимуляции.

# Направление = какие модули изменились.

# Гипотеза: у KO вектор длиннее (больший TNF-ответ) и направлен

# сторону Inflammaging/SASP (а не в сторону DDR как у WT).

# 

# 3. ДВУМЕРНЫЕ ФАЗОВЫЕ ПОРТРЕТЫ:

# DDR × Inflammaging — основная плоскость "стрессового возраста"

# Rho × SASP — плоскость "механо-воспалительного ответа"

# Каждый образец = точка + стрелка (baseline → TNF)

# =============================================================================

library(tidyverse)
library(fmsb)         \# radar chart
library(ggplot2)
library(patchwork)
library(ggrepel)

pipeline <- readRDS("output/rds/deseq2_all_results.rds")

# Фикс — vst_mat это уже матрица, не SummarizedExperiment:

vst_mat <- pipeline\$vst_mat

# Проверка:

class(vst_mat)   \# matrix / array
dim(vst_mat)     \# N генов × 14 образцов
colnames(vst_mat) \# BD01..BD57

# Вместо readRDS + assay() — берём напрямую:

vst_mat      <- pipeline$vst_mat        # матрица VST-нормализованных значений
coldata      <- pipeline$coldata        \# метаданные образцов
results_base <- pipeline$results_base   # DESeq2 results basal
results_tnf  <- pipeline$results_tnf    \# DESeq2 results TNF
all_de       <- pipeline$all_de         # объединённый DE-тиббл
sig_list     <- pipeline$sig_list       \# генсеты сигнатур
sig_scores   <- pipeline$sig_scores     # уже посчитанные скоры (если есть)
norm_counts  <- pipeline$norm_counts    \# нормализованные счёты

# Проверка размерности:

dim(vst_mat)
dim(norm_counts)
identical(colnames(vst_mat), coldata\$sample_id)  \# порядок совпадает?

# ── Загрузка генсетов модулей ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

# Предполагаем, что эти файлы существуют из предыдущих скриптов

source("data/genesets/senescence_genesets.R")

# Ожидаем: ddr_panel, inflammaging_panel, rho_panel,

# sasp_panel, proximal_tubule_panel, cgassting_panel

# Используем sig_list напрямую — он уже загружен из pipeline:

names(sig_list)

# [1] "Tyshkovskiy_DNAmAge"       "Tyshkovskiy_LongevityUp"

# [3] "Tyshkovskiy_LongevityDown" "Senescence_SASP"

# [5] "Senescence_DDR"            "Inflammaging"

# [7] "cGAS_STING"                "Rho_Activity"

# [9] "ProxTubule"                "Mito_Stress"

# [11] "sen_core"                  "sen_sasp"

# [13] "sen_ddr"                   "sen_mitochondria"

# [15] "sen_ois"

modules <- list(

# ── Сенесценция и DDR ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────

DDR           = sig_list[["Senescence_DDR"]],
SASP          = sig_list[["Senescence_SASP"]],
Sen_Core      = sen_core,          \# из senescence_genesets.R
Sen_OIS       = sen_ois,
Sen_Mito      = sen_mitochondria,

# ── Воспаление ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Inflammaging  = sig_list[["Inflammaging"]],
cGAS_STING    = sig_list[["cGAS_STING"]],

# ── Цитоскелет ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

RhoActivity   = sig_list[["Rho_Activity"]],

# ── Органо-специфические ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

ProxTubule    = sig_list[["ProxTubule"]],
Mito_Stress   = sig_list[["Mito_Stress"]],

# ── Модули Тышковского ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

Tysh_DNAmAge      = sig_list[["Tyshkovskiy_DNAmAge"]],
Tysh_LongevityUp  = sig_list[["Tyshkovskiy_LongevityUp"]],
Tysh_LongevityDown = sig_list[["Tyshkovskiy_LongevityDown"]]
)

# Проверка:

sapply(modules, length)

# Группировка для радарного графика (мета-категории)

module_categories <- c(
DDR            = "Senescence",
SASP           = "Senescence",
Sen_Core       = "Senescence",
Sen_OIS        = "Senescence",
Sen_Mito       = "Senescence",
Inflammaging   = "Inflammation",
cGAS_STING     = "Inflammation",
RhoActivity    = "Cytoskeleton",
ProxTubule     = "Organ health",
Mito_Stress    = "Mitochondria",
Tysh_DNAmAge       = "Aging clock",
Tysh_LongevityUp   = "Aging clock",
Tysh_LongevityDown = "Aging clock"
)

cat_colors <- c(
"Senescence"   = "\#E41A1C",
"Inflammation" = "\#FF7F00",
"Cytoskeleton" = "\#984EA3",
"Organ health" = "\#4DAF4A",
"Mitochondria" = "\#377EB8",
"Aging clock"  = "\#A65628"
)

# Проверка:

stopifnot(all(names(modules) %in% names(module_categories)))

# calc_score / score_signature уже есть в памяти — используем:

scores_all <- lapply(names(modules), function(mod) {
genes  <- modules[[mod]]
present <- intersect(genes, rownames(vst_mat))

if (length(present) < 3) {
message("⚠ ", mod, ": только ", length(present), " генов — пропускаем")
return(NULL)
}

mat_sub <- vst_mat[present, , drop = FALSE]

# z-score по каждому гену, потом среднее по образцу:

mat_z   <- t(scale(t(mat_sub)))
score   <- colMeans(mat_z, na.rm = TRUE)

data.frame(
sample_id = names(score),
score     = score,
module    = mod,
category  = module_categories[mod]
)
}) %>%
dplyr::bind_rows() %>%
dplyr::left_join(coldata %>% select(sample_id, genotype, group, tnf),
by = "sample_id")

# Проверка:

head(scores_all)
table(scores_all\$module)   \# каждый модуль × 14 образцов = 182 строки

# Заодно добавь удобные факторы для графиков

scores_all <- scores_all %>%
dplyr::mutate(
genotype = factor(genotype,
levels = c("WT", "PPM1A_KO", "PPM1B_KO", "Double_KO")),
tnf      = factor(tnf, levels = c("basal", "TNF12h")),
module   = factor(module, levels = names(modules)),
category = factor(category, levels = names(cat_colors))
)

# Итоговая проверка:

nrow(scores_all)               \# должно быть 13 модулей × 14 образцов = 182
dplyr::count(scores_all, module)   \# 14 строк на каждый модуль

# =============================================================================

# EXPORT + VIZ: scores_all → таблица + радар + ridge + slope

# =============================================================================

library(ggplot2)
library(ggridges)
library(fmsb)
library(patchwork)
library(scales)
theme_pub <- theme_bw()

# ── 1. ЭКСПОРТ ТАБЛИЦЫ ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────

dir.create("output/tables2", showWarnings = FALSE, recursive = TRUE)

write.csv(scores_all,
"output/tables2/module_scores_all_samples.csv",
row.names = FALSE)

# Сводная таблица: среднее ± SD по генотипу × TNF × модулю

scores_summary <- scores_all %>%
dplyr::group_by(module, category, genotype, tnf) %>%
dplyr::summarise(
mean_score = mean(score, na.rm = TRUE),
sd_score   = sd(score,  na.rm = TRUE),
n          = dplyr::n(),
.groups    = "drop"
)

write.csv(scores_summary,
"output/tables2/module_scores_summary.csv",
row.names = FALSE)

message("✓ Таблицы экспортированы")

# ── 2. ЦВЕТА ГЕНОТИПОВ ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────

geno_colors <- c(
"WT"         = "\#2166AC",
"PPM1A_KO"   = "\#D73027",
"PPM1B_KO"   = "\#F46D43",
"Double_KO"  = "\#762A83"
)

geno_order <- c("WT", "PPM1A_KO", "PPM1B_KO", "Double_KO")

# =============================================================================

# VIZ-A: РАДАРНЫЙ ГРАФИК (средние скоры по генотипам, только basal)

# =============================================================================

radar_data <- scores_summary %>%
dplyr::filter(tnf == "basal") %>%
dplyr::select(genotype, module, mean_score) %>%
tidyr::pivot_wider(names_from = module, values_from = mean_score) %>%
tibble::column_to_rownames("genotype")

# fmsb требует строки max/min первыми:

radar_max <- apply(radar_data, 2, max, na.rm = TRUE) * 1.3
radar_min <- apply(radar_data, 2, min, na.rm = TRUE) * 1.3

radar_fmsb <- rbind(radar_max, radar_min, radar_data[geno_order, ])

# Цвета с прозрачностью:

radar_cols_fill   <- adjustcolor(geno_colors[geno_order], alpha.f = 0.15)
radar_cols_border <- geno_colors[geno_order]

draw_radar <- function() {
fmsb::radarchart(
radar_fmsb,
axistype  = 1,
pcol      = radar_cols_border,
pfcol     = radar_cols_fill,
plwd      = 2.5,
plty      = 1,
cglcol    = "grey70",
cglty     = 1,
cglwd     = 0.5,
axislabcol = "grey40",
vlcex     = 0.85,
title     = "Module scores — basal (z-score mean)"
)
legend(
x = 1.1, y = 1.2,
legend  = geno_order,
col     = radar_cols_border,
lwd     = 2.5,
lty     = 1,
bty     = "n",
cex     = 0.85
)
}

png("output/figures2/VIZ_A_radar_basal.png",
width = 9, height = 8, units = "in", res = 300, bg = "white")
draw_radar()
dev.off()

pdf("output/figures2/VIZ_A_radar_basal.pdf", width = 9, height = 8)
draw_radar()
dev.off()

message("✓ VIZ-A Radar сохранён")

# =============================================================================

# VIZ-B: RIDGE PLOT — распределение скоров по модулям

# =============================================================================

# Только basal для чистоты сравнения:

p_ridge <- scores_all %>%
dplyr::filter(tnf == "basal") %>%
dplyr::mutate(
genotype = factor(genotype, levels = rev(geno_order)),
module   = factor(module,   levels = rev(levels(scores_all\$module)))
) %>%
ggplot(aes(x = score, y = module, fill = genotype, color = genotype)) +
ggridges::geom_density_ridges(
alpha = 0.55, scale = 0.85,
jittered_points = TRUE,
point_size = 1.8, point_alpha = 0.9,
position = ggridges::position_raincloud(width = 0.05, height = 0.15)
) +
scale_fill_manual(values  = geno_colors, name = "Genotype") +
scale_color_manual(values = geno_colors, name = "Genotype") +
geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed",
color = "grey40", linewidth = 0.5) +
labs(
title    = "Module score distributions — basal",
subtitle = "z-score mean across signature genes per sample",
x = "Module score (z-score)", y = NULL
) +
theme_pub +
theme(
strip.text      = element_text(size = 9),
legend.position = "right",
axis.text.y     = element_text(size = 10)
)

ggsave("output/figures2/VIZ_B_ridge_basal.png",
p_ridge, width = 11, height = 9, dpi = 300, bg = "white")
ggsave("output/figures2/VIZ_B_ridge_basal.pdf",
p_ridge, width = 11, height = 9)

message("✓ VIZ-B Ridge сохранён")

# =============================================================================

# VIZ-C: SLOPE PLOT — изменение скора basal → TNF внутри каждого генотипа

# =============================================================================

slope_data <- scores_summary %>%
dplyr::filter(genotype != "Double_KO" | tnf == "basal") %>%

# Double_KO не имеет TNF — оставляем только basal для него

dplyr::mutate(
tnf      = factor(tnf, levels = c("basal", "TNF12h")),
genotype = factor(genotype, levels = geno_order)
)

p_slope <- ggplot(slope_data,
aes(x = tnf, y = mean_score,
group = interaction(genotype, module),
color = genotype)) +
geom_line(aes(linetype = genotype), linewidth = 0.9, alpha = 0.8) +
geom_point(size = 2.5) +
geom_errorbar(aes(ymin = mean_score - sd_score,
ymax = mean_score + sd_score),
width = 0.1, alpha = 0.5) +
facet_wrap(~ module, scales = "free_y", ncol = 4) +
scale_color_manual(values = geno_colors, name = "Genotype") +
scale_linetype_manual(
values = c("WT" = "solid", "PPM1A_KO" = "dashed",
"PPM1B_KO" = "dotdash", "Double_KO" = "dotted"),
name = "Genotype"
) +
geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed",
color = "grey60", linewidth = 0.4) +
labs(
title    = "TNF effect on module scores by genotype",
subtitle = "Mean ± SD; basal → TNF12h transition",
x = NULL, y = "Module score (z-score)"
) +
theme_pub +
theme(
strip.text      = element_text(size = 8, face = "bold"),
legend.position = "bottom",
axis.text.x     = element_text(size = 9)
)

ggsave("output/figures2/VIZ_C_slope_tnf_effect.png",
p_slope, width = 14, height = 10, dpi = 300, bg = "white")
ggsave("output/figures2/VIZ_C_slope_tnf_effect.pdf",
p_slope, width = 14, height = 10)

message("✓ VIZ-C Slope сохранён")

# =============================================================================

# VIZ-D: HEATMAP скоров (все образцы × все модули)

# =============================================================================

score_mat <- scores_all %>%
dplyr::select(sample_id, module, score) %>%
tidyr::pivot_wider(names_from = module, values_from = score) %>%
tibble::column_to_rownames("sample_id") %>%
as.matrix() %>%
t()   \# модули × образцы

# Аннотация колонок:

col_ann_df <- coldata %>%
dplyr::filter(sample_id %in% colnames(score_mat)) %>%
dplyr::arrange(match(sample_id, colnames(score_mat))) %>%
dplyr::select(genotype, tnf) %>%
as.data.frame()
rownames(col_ann_df) <- colnames(score_mat)

# Аннотация строк (категории модулей):

row_ann_df <- data.frame(
category = module_categories[rownames(score_mat)],
row.names = rownames(score_mat)
)

ann_colors <- list(
genotype = geno_colors,
tnf      = c("basal" = "\#F7F7F7", "TNF12h" = "\#FC8D59"),
category = cat_colors
)

pheatmap::pheatmap(
score_mat,
annotation_col    = col_ann_df,
annotation_row    = row_ann_df,
annotation_colors = ann_colors,
color             = colorRampPalette(c("\#4575B4","white","\#D73027"))(100),
breaks            = seq(-2, 2, length.out = 101),
cluster_rows      = TRUE,
cluster_cols      = TRUE,
show_colnames     = TRUE,
fontsize          = 9,
fontsize_row      = 9,
fontsize_col      = 8,
border_color      = NA,
main              = "Module scores — all samples",
filename          = "output/figures2/VIZ_D_heatmap_scores.png",
width = 12, height = 7
)

message("✓ VIZ-D Heatmap скоров сохранён")
message("\n=== Все визуализации готовы ===")
message("Таблицы: output/tables/module_scores_*.csv")
message("Рисунки: output/figures/VIZ_[A-D]_*.png / .pdf")

# =============================================================================

# VIZ-D: HEATMAP скоров — фиксированный порядок колонок

# =============================================================================

# ── Целевой порядок групп ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

# WT_basal → PPM1A_KO_basal → PPM1B_KO_basal → Double_KO_basal → *_TNF12h

group_order <- c("WT_basal", "PPM1A_KO_basal", "PPM1B_KO_basal",
"Double_KO_basal", "WT_TNF12h", "PPM1A_KO_TNF12h",
"PPM1B_KO_TNF12h")

# Создаём ключ group для каждого образца:

sample_order <- coldata %>%
dplyr::filter(sample_id %in% colnames(score_mat)) %>%
dplyr::mutate(
grp = paste0(genotype, "_", tnf),
grp = factor(grp, levels = group_order)
) %>%
dplyr::arrange(grp, sample_id) %>%   \# внутри группы — алфавитно
dplyr::pull(sample_id)

# Переупорядочиваем матрицу:

score_mat_ord <- score_mat[, sample_order]

# Аннотация колонок (в новом порядке):

col_ann_df_ord <- coldata %>%
dplyr::filter(sample_id %in% sample_order) %>%
dplyr::arrange(match(sample_id, sample_order)) %>%
dplyr::select(genotype, tnf) %>%
dplyr::mutate(
genotype = factor(genotype, levels = c("WT","PPM1A_KO","PPM1B_KO","Double_KO")),
tnf      = factor(tnf,      levels = c("basal","TNF12h"))
) %>%
as.data.frame()
rownames(col_ann_df_ord) <- sample_order

# Аннотация строк (категории — строки кластеризуем):

row_ann_df <- data.frame(
category = module_categories[rownames(score_mat_ord)],
row.names = rownames(score_mat_ord)
)

# Разделители между группами (gaps после последнего образца каждой группы):

gap_positions <- coldata %>%
dplyr::filter(sample_id %in% sample_order) %>%
dplyr::mutate(grp = paste0(genotype, "_", tnf),
grp = factor(grp, levels = group_order)) %>%
dplyr::arrange(match(sample_id, sample_order)) %>%
dplyr::group_by(grp) %>%
dplyr::summarise(last_pos = dplyr::n(), .groups = "drop") %>%
dplyr::mutate(gap = cumsum(last_pos)) %>%
dplyr::pull(gap) %>%
head(-1)   \# убираем последний (правый край)

ann_colors <- list(
genotype = geno_colors,
tnf      = c("basal" = "\#F0F0F0", "TNF12h" = "\#FC8D59"),
category = cat_colors
)

pheatmap::pheatmap(
score_mat_ord,
annotation_col    = col_ann_df_ord,
annotation_row    = row_ann_df,
annotation_colors = ann_colors,
color             = colorRampPalette(c("\#4575B4","white","\#D73027"))(100),
breaks            = seq(-2, 2, length.out = 101),
cluster_rows      = TRUE,   \# модули кластеризуем — биологически информативно
cluster_cols      = FALSE,  \# ← колонки зафиксированы вручную
gaps_col          = gap_positions,   \# ← белые разделители между группами
show_colnames     = TRUE,
fontsize          = 9,
fontsize_row      = 9,
fontsize_col      = 7.5,
border_color      = NA,
main              = "Module scores — all samples (ordered by genotype × treatment)",
filename          = "output/figures2/VIZ_D_heatmap_scores2.png",
width = 13, height = 7
)

message("✓ VIZ-D Heatmap (фиксированный порядок) сохранён")

# =============================================================================

# VIZ-D v2: Яркая палитра — три варианта (раскомментируй нужный)

# =============================================================================

# ── Вариант 1: RdBu reversed (классика, максимальный контраст) ───────────────

my_palette <- rev(RColorBrewer::brewer.pal(11, "RdBu"))

# Интерполируем до 100 цветов:

pal100 <- colorRampPalette(my_palette)(100)

# ── Симметричные breaks вокруг нуля ─────────────────────────────────────────

# Смотрим реальный диапазон скоров:

score_range <- max(abs(range(score_mat_ord, na.rm = TRUE)))
score_range <- ceiling(score_range * 10) / 10  \# округляем вверх до 0.1

my_breaks <- seq(-score_range, score_range, length.out = 101)

# ── Финальный heatmap ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

pheatmap::pheatmap(
score_mat_ord,
annotation_col    = col_ann_df_ord,
annotation_row    = row_ann_df,
annotation_colors = ann_colors,
color             = pal100,
breaks            = my_breaks,
cluster_rows      = TRUE,
cluster_cols      = FALSE,
gaps_col          = gap_positions,
show_colnames     = TRUE,
fontsize          = 9,
fontsize_row      = 9,
fontsize_col      = 7.5,
border_color      = NA,

# ── Доп. настройки для яркости ───────────────────────────────────────────

cellwidth         = 22,   \# шире ячейки → насыщеннее цвет визуально
cellheight        = 18,
main              = "Module scores — all samples",
filename          = "output/figures2/VIZ_D_heatmap_scores3.png",
width = 14, height = 7
)

message("✓ VIZ-D v2 (яркая палитра) сохранён")

# ── РИСУНОК B: Фазовые портреты с TNF-траекторией ────────────────────────────

# DDR × Inflammaging — основная плоскость

# Каждый образец — точка; стрелка = направление при добавлении TNF

# Средние ctrl + TNF для каждого генотипа с TNF-образцом

phase_data <- mod_scores %>%
dplyr::filter(module %in% c("DDR","Inflammaging")) %>%
pivot_wider(names_from = module, values_from = score) %>%
group_by(genotype, tnf) %>%
summarise(
DDR_mean = mean(DDR, na.rm=TRUE),
Inf_mean = mean(Inflammaging, na.rm=TRUE),
.groups  = "drop"
) %>%
pivot_wider(names_from = tnf,
values_from = c(DDR_mean, Inf_mean))

# Шаг 1: смотрим что реально получилось после pivot_wider

phase_data <- scores_all %>%
dplyr::filter(module %in% c("DDR", "Inflammaging")) %>%
tidyr::pivot_wider(names_from = module, values_from = score) %>%
dplyr::group_by(genotype, tnf) %>%
dplyr::summarise(
DDR_mean = mean(DDR,          na.rm = TRUE),
Inf_mean = mean(Inflammaging, na.rm = TRUE),
.groups  = "drop"
) %>%
tidyr::pivot_wider(
names_from  = tnf,
values_from = c(DDR_mean, Inf_mean)
)

# Смотрим реальные имена колонок:

colnames(phase_data)

# Скорее всего: "genotype" "DDR_mean_basal" "DDR_mean_TNF12h"

# "Inf_mean_basal" "Inf_mean_TNF12h"

# Шаг 2: стрелки basal → TNF12h

phase_arrows <- phase_data %>%
dplyr::filter(!is.na(DDR_mean_TNF12h)) %>%   \# ← TNF12h, не tnf
dplyr::mutate(
genotype = factor(genotype, levels = c("WT", "PPM1A_KO", "PPM1B_KO"))
\# Double_KO выпадет сам — у него нет TNF12h
)

# Шаг 3: фазовый портрет

p_phase <- ggplot() +

# Точки basal:

geom_point(data = phase_arrows,
aes(x = DDR_mean_basal, y = Inf_mean_basal,
color = genotype),
size = 4, shape = 16) +

# Точки Double_KO (только basal, без стрелки):

geom_point(data = phase_data %>% dplyr::filter(genotype == "Double_KO"),
aes(x = DDR_mean_basal, y = Inf_mean_basal),
color = geno_colors["Double_KO"],
size = 4, shape = 17) +   \# треугольник — нет TNF

# Стрелки basal → TNF12h:

geom_segment(data = phase_arrows,
aes(x    = DDR_mean_basal,   y    = Inf_mean_basal,
xend = DDR_mean_TNF12h,  yend = Inf_mean_TNF12h,
color = genotype),
arrow = arrow(length = unit(0.25, "cm"), type = "closed"),
linewidth = 1.2) +

# Точки TNF12h (конец стрелки):

geom_point(data = phase_arrows,
aes(x = DDR_mean_TNF12h, y = Inf_mean_TNF12h,
color = genotype),
size = 3, shape = 1, stroke = 1.2) +   \# открытый круг

# Подписи генотипов у базальных точек:

ggrepel::geom_label_repel(
data = phase_data,
aes(x = DDR_mean_basal, y = Inf_mean_basal,
label = genotype, color = genotype),
size = 3.2, show.legend = FALSE,
box.padding = 0.4, seed = 42
) +
scale_color_manual(values = geno_colors, name = "Genotype") +
geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed", color = "grey60") +
geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed", color = "grey60") +
labs(
title    = "Phase portrait: DDR × Inflammaging",
subtitle = "Filled circle = basal; open circle = TNF12h; arrow = trajectory",
x = "DDR module score (z-score)",
y = "Inflammaging module score (z-score)"
) +
theme_pub

ggsave("output/figures2/VIZ_B_phase_DDR_Inflammaging.png",
p_phase, width = 7, height = 6, dpi = 300, bg = "white")
ggsave("output/figures2/VIZ_B_phase_DDR_Inflammaging.pdf",
p_phase, width = 7, height = 6)

message("✓ VIZ-B Phase portrait сохранён")

# Аналогичный фазовый портрет Rho × SASP

p_rho_sasp <- mod_scores %>%
dplyr::filter(module %in% c("RhoActivity","SASP")) %>%
pivot_wider(names_from=module, values_from=score) %>%
dplyr::mutate(genotype  = factor(genotype, levels=c("WT","WipKO","Ppm1b_KO","Double_KO")),
tnf_label = ifelse(tnf=="tnf","TNF 12h","Baseline")) %>%
ggplot(aes(x=RhoActivity, y=SASP,
color=genotype, shape=tnf_label)) +
geom_hline(yintercept=0, linetype="dashed", color="grey70") +
geom_vline(xintercept=0, linetype="dashed", color="grey70") +
geom_point(size=4, alpha=0.85) +
geom_text_repel(aes(label=sample_id), size=2.8, max.overlaps=15,
segment.color="grey70") +
scale_color_manual(values=GENO_COLORS) +
scale_shape_manual(values=c("Baseline"=21,"TNF 12h"=24), name="Stimulation") +
labs(title    = "Phase portrait: Rho GTPase × SASP",
subtitle = "Double_KO position: additive or synergistic?",
x="RhoActivity score", y="SASP score", color="Genotype") +
theme_bw(base_size=11) +
theme(legend.position="right", panel.grid.minor=element_blank())

ggsave("output/figures2/BIOINF_phase_Rho_SASP.pdf",
p_rho_sasp, width=9, height=7)
ggsave("output/figures2/BIOINF_phase_Rho_SASP.png",
p_rho_sasp, width=9, height=7, dpi=300)

message("✓ Module clocks COMPLETE")

# =============================================================================

# PHASE PORTRAIT: RhoActivity × SASP

# =============================================================================

# ── Данные ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

phase_rho_sasp <- scores_all %>%
dplyr::filter(module %in% c("RhoActivity", "SASP")) %>%
tidyr::pivot_wider(names_from = module, values_from = score) %>%
dplyr::group_by(genotype, tnf) %>%
dplyr::summarise(
Rho_mean  = mean(RhoActivity, na.rm = TRUE),
SASP_mean = mean(SASP,        na.rm = TRUE),
.groups   = "drop"
) %>%
tidyr::pivot_wider(
names_from  = tnf,
values_from = c(Rho_mean, SASP_mean)
)

colnames(phase_rho_sasp)  \# проверка: Rho_mean_basal, Rho_mean_TNF12h, ...

# Генотипы с TNF-образцами (для стрелок):

arrows_rho_sasp <- phase_rho_sasp %>%
dplyr::filter(!is.na(Rho_mean_TNF12h)) %>%
dplyr::mutate(genotype = factor(genotype, levels = geno_order))

# Double_KO — только basal, без стрелки:

dko_point <- phase_rho_sasp %>%
dplyr::filter(genotype == "Double_KO")

# ── График ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

p_phase_rho <- ggplot() +

# Фоновые квадранты — подписи биологического смысла:

annotate("text", x = -Inf, y =  Inf, label = "Low Rho\nHigh SASP",
hjust = -0.1, vjust = 1.3, size = 2.8, color = "grey60", fontface = "italic") +
annotate("text", x =  Inf, y =  Inf, label = "High Rho\nHigh SASP",
hjust = 1.1,  vjust = 1.3, size = 2.8, color = "\#B2182B", fontface = "bold.italic") +
annotate("text", x = -Inf, y = -Inf, label = "Low Rho\nLow SASP",
hjust = -0.1, vjust = -0.3, size = 2.8, color = "grey60", fontface = "italic") +
annotate("text", x =  Inf, y = -Inf, label = "High Rho\nLow SASP",
hjust = 1.1,  vjust = -0.3, size = 2.8, color = "grey50", fontface = "italic") +

# Крест нулей:

geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed", color = "grey70", linewidth = 0.5) +
geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed", color = "grey70", linewidth = 0.5) +

# Стрелки basal → TNF12h:

geom_segment(
data = arrows_rho_sasp,
aes(x    = Rho_mean_basal,   y    = SASP_mean_basal,
xend = Rho_mean_TNF12h,  yend = SASP_mean_TNF12h,
color = genotype),
arrow     = arrow(length = unit(0.28, "cm"), type = "closed"),
linewidth = 1.3, alpha = 0.85
) +

# Точки basal (генотипы со стрелками):

geom_point(
data = arrows_rho_sasp,
aes(x = Rho_mean_basal, y = SASP_mean_basal, color = genotype),
size = 5, shape = 16
) +

# Точки TNF12h (конец стрелки):

geom_point(
data = arrows_rho_sasp,
aes(x = Rho_mean_TNF12h, y = SASP_mean_TNF12h, color = genotype),
size = 3.5, shape = 1, stroke = 1.5
) +

# Double_KO — только basal, треугольник:

geom_point(
data = dko_point,
aes(x = Rho_mean_basal, y = SASP_mean_basal),
color = geno_colors["Double_KO"],
size = 5, shape = 17
) +

# Подписи всех генотипов:

ggrepel::geom_label_repel(
data = phase_rho_sasp,
aes(x     = Rho_mean_basal,
y     = SASP_mean_basal,
label = genotype,
color = genotype),
size          = 3.2,
label.padding = unit(0.2, "lines"),
box.padding   = 0.5,
show.legend   = FALSE,
seed          = 7
) +

# Легенда формы:

annotate("text", x = Inf, y = -Inf,
label = "● basal   ○ TNF12h   ▲ basal only",
hjust = 1.05, vjust = -0.5,
size = 2.6, color = "grey40") +

scale_color_manual(values = geno_colors, name = "Genotype") +
coord_cartesian(clip = "off") +
labs(
title    = "Phase portrait: RhoActivity × SASP",
subtitle = "Filled circle = basal; open circle = TNF12h; arrow = trajectory\nTriangle = basal only (no TNF data)",
x = "Rho Activity module score (z-score)",
y = "SASP module score (z-score)"
) +
theme_pub +
theme(
plot.margin   = margin(10, 20, 10, 10),
legend.position = "right"
)

ggsave("output/figures2/VIZ_B2_phase_Rho_SASP.png",
p_phase_rho, width = 7.5, height = 6.5, dpi = 300, bg = "white")
ggsave("output/figures2/VIZ_B2_phase_Rho_SASP.pdf",
p_phase_rho, width = 7.5, height = 6.5)

message("✓ VIZ-B2 Phase portrait Rho×SASP сохранён")

# =============================================================================

# ЭКСПОРТ ТАБЛИЧНЫХ ДАННЫХ ДЛЯ PHASE PORTRAITS

# =============================================================================

dir.create("output/tables2", showWarnings = FALSE, recursive = TRUE)

# ── Phase DDR × Inflammaging ─────────────────────────────────────────────────

write.csv(phase_data,
"output/tables2/phase_DDR_Inflammaging.csv",
row.names = FALSE)

# ── Phase Rho × SASP ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

write.csv(phase_rho_sasp,
"output/tables2/phase_Rho_SASP.csv",
row.names = FALSE)

message("✓ Таблицы phase portraits экспортированы")

Вот полностью переписанный скрипт 04 с учётом всех реальных данных из coldata (`PPM1D_KO`, `DKO`, `PPM1B_KO`):

```r
# =============================================================================
# 04_module_clocks_v3.R
#
# БИОЛОГИЧЕСКИЙ СМЫСЛ:
#   "Module clocks" — многомерные биологические часы:
#   DDR, Inflammaging, Rho, SASP, ProxTubule и др. как спицы радара.
#   Позволяет увидеть ПРОФИЛЬ состояния клетки целиком.
#
#   ВОПРОСЫ:
#   1. DOUBLE KO (DKO): синергия vs. аддитивность vs. компенсация?
#   2. TNF-ТРАЕКТОРИЯ: длина и направление вектора basal→TNF12h
#      (гипотеза: у KO вектор длиннее, направлен в сторону SASP)
#   3. ФАЗОВЫЕ ПОРТРЕТЫ: DDR×Inflammaging и Rho×SASP
#
# ИСПРАВЛЕНИЯ v3:
#   - PPM1D_KO / DKO / PPM1B_KO — реальные имена из coldata
#   - group_order использует реальные уровни: DKO_basal, PPM1D_KO_basal, etc.
#   - убран mod_scores (не определён), везде scores_all
#   - phase_data: правильные имена колонок после pivot_wider
#   - убраны GENO_COLORS / WipKO / Double_KO
#   - score_signature определена внутри скрипта (не зависит от 03)
# =============================================================================

suppressPackageStartupMessages({
  library(tidyverse)
  library(fmsb)
  library(ggrepel)
  library(patchwork)
  library(ggridges)
  library(pheatmap)
  library(RColorBrewer)
  library(scales)
})

# =============================================================================
# 0. Создаём папки
# =============================================================================
dir.create("output/figures/module_clocks", recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)
dir.create("output/tables",               recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)

# =============================================================================
# 1. Загружаем pipeline
# =============================================================================
pipeline <- readRDS("output/rds/deseq2_all_results.rds")

vst_mat  <- as.matrix(pipeline$norm_counts)   # матрица VST: гены × образцы
coldata  <- pipeline$coldata                   # tibble: sample_id, genotype, tnf, group, ...
sig_list <- pipeline$sig_list                  # генсеты из 02/03 скриптов

message("✓ vst_mat: ", nrow(vst_mat), " генов × ", ncol(vst_mat), " образцов")
message("✓ sig_list генсеты: ", paste(names(sig_list), collapse = ", "))

# Упорядочиваем столбцы матрицы по coldata
stopifnot(all(coldata$sample_id %in% colnames(vst_mat)))
vst_mat <- vst_mat[, coldata$sample_id]

# =============================================================================
# 2. Реальные уровни факторов (из coldata)
# =============================================================================
# genotype: "WT" "PPM1D_KO" "PPM1B_KO" "DKO"
# group:    "WT_basal" "PPM1D_KO_basal" "PPM1B_KO_basal" "DKO_basal"
#           "WT_TNF12h" "PPM1D_KO_TNF12h" "PPM1B_KO_TNF12h"
# tnf:      "basal" "TNF12h"

geno_order  <- c("WT", "PPM1D_KO", "PPM1B_KO", "DKO")
group_order <- c(
  "WT_basal", "PPM1D_KO_basal", "PPM1B_KO_basal", "DKO_basal",
  "WT_TNF12h", "PPM1D_KO_TNF12h", "PPM1B_KO_TNF12h"
)

geno_colors <- c(
  "WT"       = "#2166AC",
  "PPM1D_KO" = "#D73027",
  "PPM1B_KO" = "#F46D43",
  "DKO"      = "#762A83"
)

cat_colors <- c(
  "Senescence"   = "#E41A1C",
  "Inflammation" = "#FF7F00",
  "Cytoskeleton" = "#984EA3",
  "Organ health" = "#4DAF4A",
  "Mitochondria" = "#377EB8",
  "Aging clock"  = "#A65628",
  "Other"        = "#CCCCCC"
)

theme_pub <- theme_bw(base_size = 11) +
  theme(panel.grid.minor = element_blank())

# =============================================================================
# 3. Модули: берём из sig_list + добавляем кастомные сенесцентные
# =============================================================================

# Загружаем кастомные генсеты из 03 скрипта если они сохранены
sen_gs_path <- "data/genesets/senescence_genesets.rds"
if (file.exists(sen_gs_path)) {
  sen_gs <- readRDS(sen_gs_path)
} else {
  sen_gs <- list()
  message("⚠ senescence_genesets.rds не найден — используем только sig_list")
}

# Объединяем: sig_list имеет приоритет
all_gs <- c(sen_gs, sig_list)
all_gs <- all_gs[!duplicated(names(all_gs))]   # убираем дубликаты (приоритет sig_list)

message("✓ Всего генсетов для скоринга: ", length(all_gs))

# Определяем рабочие модули — берём что есть
module_candidates <- c(
  "Senescence_DDR", "sen_ddr",
  "Senescence_SASP", "sen_sasp",
  "sen_core",
  "sen_ois",
  "sen_mitochondria",
  "Inflammaging",
  "cGAS_STING",
  "Rho_Activity",
  "ProxTubule",
  "Mito_Stress",
  "Tyshkovskiy_DNAmAge",   "Aging_DNAmAge",
  "Tyshkovskiy_LongevityUp",   "Aging_LongevityUp",
  "Tyshkovskiy_LongevityDown", "Aging_LongevityDown"
)

# Берём первый найденный синоним для каждого модуля
module_alias <- list(
  DDR            = c("Senescence_DDR",  "sen_ddr"),
  SASP           = c("Senescence_SASP", "sen_sasp"),
  Sen_Core       = "sen_core",
  Sen_OIS        = "sen_ois",
  Sen_Mito       = "sen_mitochondria",
  Inflammaging   = "Inflammaging",
  cGAS_STING     = "cGAS_STING",
  RhoActivity    = "Rho_Activity",
  ProxTubule     = "ProxTubule",
  Mito_Stress    = "Mito_Stress",
  Tysh_DNAmAge       = c("Tyshkovskiy_DNAmAge",      "Aging_DNAmAge"),
  Tysh_LongevityUp   = c("Tyshkovskiy_LongevityUp",  "Aging_LongevityUp"),
  Tysh_LongevityDown = c("Tyshkovskiy_LongevityDown","Aging_LongevityDown")
)

modules <- list()
for (mod_name in names(module_alias)) {
  for (alias in module_alias[[mod_name]]) {
    if (alias %in% names(all_gs)) {
      modules[[mod_name]] <- all_gs[[alias]]
      break
    }
  }
}

# Убираем не найденные
modules <- Filter(Negate(is.null), modules)
message("✓ Найдено рабочих модулей: ", length(modules), ": ",
        paste(names(modules), collapse = ", "))

# Категории для каждого модуля
module_categories <- c(
  DDR            = "Senescence",
  SASP           = "Senescence",
  Sen_Core       = "Senescence",
  Sen_OIS        = "Senescence",
  Sen_Mito       = "Senescence",
  Inflammaging   = "Inflammation",
  cGAS_STING     = "Inflammation",
  RhoActivity    = "Cytoskeleton",
  ProxTubule     = "Organ health",
  Mito_Stress    = "Mitochondria",
  Tysh_DNAmAge       = "Aging clock",
  Tysh_LongevityUp   = "Aging clock",
  Tysh_LongevityDown = "Aging clock"
)

# =============================================================================
# 4. Z-score нормализация матрицы и скоринг модулей
# =============================================================================
vst_z <- t(scale(t(vst_mat)))

# Функция скоринга (средний z-score по генсету)
score_signature_local <- function(mat_z, geneset, sig_name) {
  genes_found <- intersect(geneset, rownames(mat_z))
  if (length(genes_found) < 3) {
    message("⚠ ", sig_name, ": только ", length(genes_found),
            " генов в матрице — пропускаем")
    return(NULL)
  }
  scores <- colMeans(mat_z[genes_found, , drop = FALSE], na.rm = TRUE)
  tibble(
    sample_id = names(scores),
    score     = as.numeric(scores),
    module    = sig_name,
    n_genes   = length(genes_found)
  )
}

# Считаем скоры для всех модулей
scores_raw <- map_dfr(names(modules),
                      ~ score_signature_local(vst_z, modules[[.x]], .x))

message("✓ Скоры посчитаны: ", nrow(scores_raw), " строк")

# =============================================================================
# 5. Join с coldata
# =============================================================================
scores_all <- scores_raw %>%
  left_join(
    coldata %>%
      select(sample_id, genotype, tnf, group,
             any_of(c("n_replicates", "exploratory"))),
    by = "sample_id"
  ) %>%
  mutate(
    genotype = factor(genotype, levels = geno_order),
    tnf      = factor(tnf,      levels = c("basal", "TNF12h")),
    module   = factor(module,   levels = names(modules)),
    category = factor(
      module_categories[as.character(module)],
      levels = names(cat_colors)
    )
  )

# Диагностика
message("\n── Проверка scores_all ──────────────────────────────────")
message("  Строк: ", nrow(scores_all))
message("  NA в genotype: ", sum(is.na(scores_all$genotype)))
message("  NA в tnf: ",      sum(is.na(scores_all$tnf)))
print(count(scores_all, module))

stopifnot(
  "NA в genotype" = sum(is.na(scores_all$genotype)) == 0,
  "NA в tnf"      = sum(is.na(scores_all$tnf))      == 0
)

# Экспорт
write_csv(scores_all, "output/tables/module_scores_all_samples.csv")

# =============================================================================
# 6. Сводная таблица mean ± SD
# =============================================================================
scores_summary <- scores_all %>%
  group_by(module, category, genotype, tnf) %>%
  summarise(
    mean_score = mean(score, na.rm = TRUE),
    sd_score   = sd(score,  na.rm = TRUE),
    n          = n(),
    .groups    = "drop"
  )

write_csv(scores_summary, "output/tables/module_scores_summary.csv")
message("✓ Таблицы экспортированы")

# =============================================================================
# 7. VIZ-A: Радарный график (basal, средние по генотипу)
# =============================================================================

# Оставляем только модули с достаточным числом генов (уже отфильтровано)
radar_data <- scores_summary %>%
  filter(tnf == "basal") %>%
  select(genotype, module, mean_score) %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = module, values_from = mean_score) %>%
  column_to_rownames("genotype")

# DKO может отсутствовать в geno_order если нет basal — проверяем
geno_in_radar <- intersect(geno_order, rownames(radar_data))

radar_max <- apply(radar_data, 2, max, na.rm = TRUE) * 1.3
radar_min <- apply(radar_data, 2, min, na.rm = TRUE) * 1.3
radar_fmsb <- rbind(radar_max, radar_min, radar_data[geno_in_radar, ])

radar_cols_border <- geno_colors[geno_in_radar]
radar_cols_fill   <- adjustcolor(radar_cols_border, alpha.f = 0.15)

draw_radar <- function() {
  par(mar = c(2, 2, 3, 2))
  fmsb::radarchart(
    radar_fmsb,
    axistype   = 1,
    pcol       = radar_cols_border,
    pfcol      = radar_cols_fill,
    plwd       = 2.5,
    plty       = 1,
    cglcol     = "grey70",
    cglty      = 1,
    cglwd      = 0.5,
    axislabcol = "grey40",
    vlcex      = 0.78,
    title      = "Module scores — basal (mean z-score)"
  )
  legend(
    x      = 1.15, y = 1.25,
    legend = geno_in_radar,
    col    = radar_cols_border,
    lwd    = 2.5, lty = 1,
    bty    = "n", cex = 0.85
  )
}

png("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_A_radar_basal.png",
    width = 9, height = 8, units = "in", res = 300, bg = "white")
draw_radar()
dev.off()

pdf("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_A_radar_basal.pdf",
    width = 9, height = 8)
draw_radar()
dev.off()

message("✓ VIZ-A Radar сохранён")

# =============================================================================
# 8. VIZ-B: Ridge plot — распределение скоров, только basal
# =============================================================================
p_ridge <- scores_all %>%
  filter(tnf == "basal") %>%
  mutate(
    genotype = factor(genotype, levels = rev(geno_order)),
    module   = factor(module,   levels = rev(levels(scores_all$module)))
  ) %>%
  ggplot(aes(x = score, y = module,
             fill = genotype, color = genotype)) +
  ggridges::geom_density_ridges(
    alpha           = 0.55,
    scale           = 0.85,
    jittered_points = TRUE,
    point_size      = 2,
    point_alpha     = 0.9,
    position        = ggridges::position_raincloud(
      width  = 0.05,
      height = 0.15
    )
  ) +
  scale_fill_manual(values  = geno_colors, name = "Genotype") +
  scale_color_manual(values = geno_colors, name = "Genotype") +
  geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed",
             color = "grey40", linewidth = 0.5) +
  labs(
    title    = "Module score distributions — basal",
    subtitle = "Mean z-score across signature genes | MC38 cells",
    x = "Module score (z-score)", y = NULL
  ) +
  theme_pub +
  theme(
    legend.position = "right",
    axis.text.y     = element_text(size = 10)
  )

ggsave("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_B_ridge_basal.png",
       p_ridge, width = 11, height = 9, dpi = 300, bg = "white")
ggsave("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_B_ridge_basal.pdf",
       p_ridge, width = 11, height = 9)

message("✓ VIZ-B Ridge сохранён")

# =============================================================================
# 9. VIZ-C: Slope plot — basal → TNF12h по генотипам
# =============================================================================
# DKO не имеет TNF-образца, поэтому для него только basal-точка
slope_data <- scores_summary %>%
  mutate(
    tnf      = factor(tnf, levels = c("basal", "TNF12h")),
    genotype = factor(genotype, levels = geno_order)
  )

p_slope <- ggplot(slope_data,
                  aes(x     = tnf,
                      y     = mean_score,
                      group = interaction(genotype, module),
                      color = genotype)) +
  geom_line(aes(linetype = genotype), linewidth = 0.9, alpha = 0.85) +
  geom_point(size = 2.5) +
  geom_errorbar(
    aes(ymin = mean_score - sd_score,
        ymax = mean_score + sd_score),
    width = 0.1, alpha = 0.5
  ) +
  facet_wrap(~ module, scales = "free_y", ncol = 4) +
  scale_color_manual(values = geno_colors, name = "Genotype") +
  scale_linetype_manual(
    values = c("WT"       = "solid",
               "PPM1D_KO" = "dashed",
               "PPM1B_KO" = "dotdash",
               "DKO"      = "dotted"),
    name = "Genotype"
  ) +
  geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed",
             color = "grey60", linewidth = 0.4) +
  labs(
    title    = "TNF effect on module scores by genotype",
    subtitle = "Mean ± SD; basal → TNF12h | DKO: basal only",
    x = NULL, y = "Module score (z-score)"
  ) +
  theme_pub +
  theme(
    strip.text      = element_text(size = 8, face = "bold"),
    strip.background = element_rect(fill = "grey92"),
    legend.position = "bottom",
    axis.text.x     = element_text(size = 9)
  )

ggsave("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_C_slope_tnf_effect.png",
       p_slope, width = 14, height = 10, dpi = 300, bg = "white")
ggsave("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_C_slope_tnf_effect.pdf",
       p_slope, width = 14, height = 10)

message("✓ VIZ-C Slope сохранён")

# =============================================================================
# 10. VIZ-D: Heatmap всех скоров — фиксированный порядок колонок
# =============================================================================
score_mat <- scores_all %>%
  select(sample_id, module, score) %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = module, values_from = score) %>%
  column_to_rownames("sample_id") %>%
  as.matrix() %>%
  t()   # модули × образцы

# Порядок образцов по группам
sample_order_df <- coldata %>%
  filter(sample_id %in% colnames(score_mat)) %>%
  mutate(group = factor(group, levels = group_order)) %>%
  arrange(group, sample_id)

sample_order <- sample_order_df$sample_id
score_mat_ord <- score_mat[, sample_order]

# Аннотация столбцов
col_ann_df <- sample_order_df %>%
  select(genotype, tnf) %>%
  mutate(
    genotype = factor(genotype, levels = geno_order),
    tnf      = factor(tnf,      levels = c("basal", "TNF12h"))
  ) %>%
  as.data.frame()
rownames(col_ann_df) <- sample_order

# Аннотация строк
row_ann_df <- data.frame(
  category = module_categories[rownames(score_mat_ord)],
  row.names = rownames(score_mat_ord)
)
row_ann_df$category[is.na(row_ann_df$category)] <- "Other"

# Разделители между группами
gap_positions <- sample_order_df %>%
  mutate(grp = as.character(group)) %>%
  group_by(grp) %>%
  summarise(n = n(), .groups = "drop") %>%
  # сохраняем порядок group_order
  slice(match(intersect(group_order, unique(grp)), grp)) %>%
  mutate(gap = cumsum(n)) %>%
  pull(gap) %>%
  head(-1)

# Цвета аннотаций — именованные векторы
used_cat   <- unique(row_ann_df$category)
ann_colors <- list(
  genotype = geno_colors[geno_order],
  tnf      = c("basal" = "#F0F0F0", "TNF12h" = "#FC8D59"),
  category = cat_colors[used_cat]
)

# Палитра heatmap
score_range <- max(abs(range(score_mat_ord, na.rm = TRUE)), na.rm = TRUE)
score_range <- ceiling(score_range * 10) / 10
pal100      <- colorRampPalette(rev(brewer.pal(11, "RdBu")))(100)
my_breaks   <- seq(-score_range, score_range, length.out = 101)

pheatmap::pheatmap(
  score_mat_ord,
  annotation_col    = col_ann_df,
  annotation_row    = row_ann_df,
  annotation_colors = ann_colors,
  color             = pal100,
  breaks            = my_breaks,
  cluster_rows      = TRUE,
  cluster_cols      = FALSE,
  gaps_col          = gap_positions,
  show_colnames     = TRUE,
  cellwidth         = 22,
  cellheight        = 18,
  fontsize          = 9,
  fontsize_row      = 9,
  fontsize_col      = 7.5,
  border_color      = NA,
  main              = "Module scores — all samples (ordered by genotype × treatment)",
  filename          = "output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_D_heatmap_scores.png",
  width = 14, height = 7
)

message("✓ VIZ-D Heatmap сохранён")

# =============================================================================
# 11. VIZ-E: Фазовый портрет DDR × Inflammaging
# =============================================================================

# Проверяем наличие обоих модулей
if (all(c("DDR", "Inflammaging") %in% names(modules))) {

  phase_ddr <- scores_all %>%
    filter(module %in% c("DDR", "Inflammaging")) %>%
    pivot_wider(names_from = module, values_from = score) %>%
    group_by(genotype, tnf) %>%
    summarise(
      DDR_mean = mean(DDR,          na.rm = TRUE),
      Inf_mean = mean(Inflammaging, na.rm = TRUE),
      .groups  = "drop"
    ) %>%
    pivot_wider(
      names_from  = tnf,
      values_from = c(DDR_mean, Inf_mean)
    )

  # Реальные имена колонок: DDR_mean_basal, DDR_mean_TNF12h, Inf_mean_basal, Inf_mean_TNF12h
  message("Колонки phase_ddr: ", paste(names(phase_ddr), collapse = ", "))

  # Генотипы с TNF-данными (WT, PPM1D_KO, PPM1B_KO)
  arrows_ddr <- phase_ddr %>%
    filter(!is.na(DDR_mean_TNF12h)) %>%
    mutate(genotype = factor(genotype, levels = geno_order))

  # DKO — только basal
  dko_ddr <- phase_ddr %>%
    filter(genotype == "DKO")

  p_phase_ddr <- ggplot() +
    geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed",
               color = "grey70", linewidth = 0.5) +
    geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed",
               color = "grey70", linewidth = 0.5) +
    # Стрелки basal → TNF12h
    geom_segment(
      data = arrows_ddr,
      aes(x    = DDR_mean_basal, y    = Inf_mean_basal,
          xend = DDR_mean_TNF12h, yend = Inf_mean_TNF12h,
          color = genotype),
      arrow     = arrow(length = unit(0.28, "cm"), type = "closed"),
      linewidth = 1.3, alpha = 0.85
    ) +
    # Точки basal (генотипы со стрелками)
    geom_point(
      data = arrows_ddr,
      aes(x = DDR_mean_basal, y = Inf_mean_basal, color = genotype),
      size = 5, shape = 16
    ) +
    # Точки TNF12h (конец стрелки)
    geom_point(
      data = arrows_ddr,
      aes(x = DDR_mean_TNF12h, y = Inf_mean_TNF12h, color = genotype),
      size = 3.5, shape = 1, stroke = 1.5
    ) +
    # DKO — треугольник, только basal
    geom_point(
      data  = dko_ddr,
      aes(x = DDR_mean_basal, y = Inf_mean_basal),
      color = geno_colors["DKO"],
      size  = 5, shape = 17
    ) +
    # Подписи
    ggrepel::geom_label_repel(
      data = phase_ddr,
      aes(x     = DDR_mean_basal,
          y     = Inf_mean_basal,
          label = genotype,
          color = genotype),
      size          = 3.2,
      box.padding   = 0.5,
      show.legend   = FALSE,
      seed          = 42
    ) +
    annotate("text", x = Inf, y = -Inf,
             label = "● basal   ○ TNF12h   ▲ DKO basal only",
             hjust = 1.05, vjust = -0.5,
             size = 2.6, color = "grey40") +
    scale_color_manual(values = geno_colors, name = "Genotype") +
    coord_cartesian(clip = "off") +
    labs(
      title    = "Phase portrait: DDR × Inflammaging",
      subtitle = "● basal  ○ TNF12h  ▲ DKO (no TNF data) | MC38",
      x = "DDR module score (z-score)",
      y = "Inflammaging module score (z-score)"
    ) +
    theme_pub +
    theme(plot.margin = margin(10, 25, 10, 10))

  ggsave("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_E_phase_DDR_Inflammaging.png",
         p_phase_ddr, width = 7, height = 6, dpi = 300, bg = "white")
  ggsave("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_E_phase_DDR_Inflammaging.pdf",
         p_phase_ddr, width = 7, height = 6)

  write_csv(phase_ddr, "output/tables/phase_DDR_Inflammaging.csv")
  message("✓ VIZ-E Phase DDR×Inflammaging сохранён")

} else {
  message("⚠ VIZ-E пропущен: DDR или Inflammaging не найдены в modules")
}

# =============================================================================
# 12. VIZ-F: Фазовый портрет RhoActivity × SASP
# =============================================================================

if (all(c("RhoActivity", "SASP") %in% names(modules))) {

  phase_rho <- scores_all %>%
    filter(module %in% c("RhoActivity", "SASP")) %>%
    pivot_wider(names_from = module, values_from = score) %>%
    group_by(genotype, tnf) %>%
    summarise(
      Rho_mean  = mean(RhoActivity, na.rm = TRUE),
      SASP_mean = mean(SASP,        na.rm = TRUE),
      .groups   = "drop"
    ) %>%
    pivot_wider(
      names_from  = tnf,
      values_from = c(Rho_mean, SASP_mean)
    )

  message("Колонки phase_rho: ", paste(names(phase_rho), collapse = ", "))

  arrows_rho <- phase_rho %>%
    filter(!is.na(Rho_mean_TNF12h)) %>%
    mutate(genotype = factor(genotype, levels = geno_order))

  dko_rho <- phase_rho %>%
    filter(genotype == "DKO")

  p_phase_rho <- ggplot() +
    # Квадранты — биологические метки
    annotate("text", x = -Inf, y =  Inf,
             label = "Low Rho\nHigh SASP",
             hjust = -0.1, vjust = 1.3,
             size = 2.8, color = "grey60", fontface = "italic") +
    annotate("text", x =  Inf, y =  Inf,
             label = "High Rho\nHigh SASP",
             hjust = 1.1, vjust = 1.3,
             size = 2.8, color = "#B2182B", fontface = "bold.italic") +
    annotate("text", x = -Inf, y = -Inf,
             label = "Low Rho\nLow SASP",
             hjust = -0.1, vjust = -0.3,
             size = 2.8, color = "grey60", fontface = "italic") +
    annotate("text", x =  Inf, y = -Inf,
             label = "High Rho\nLow SASP",
             hjust = 1.1, vjust = -0.3,
             size = 2.8, color = "grey50", fontface = "italic") +
    geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed",
               color = "grey70", linewidth = 0.5) +
    geom_vline(xintercept = 0, linetype = "dashed",
               color = "grey70", linewidth = 0.5) +
    # Стрелки
    geom_segment(
      data = arrows_rho,
      aes(x    = Rho_mean_basal,  y    = SASP_mean_basal,
          xend = Rho_mean_TNF12h, yend = SASP_mean_TNF12h,
          color = genotype),
      arrow     = arrow(length = unit(0.28, "cm"), type = "closed"),
      linewidth = 1.3, alpha = 0.85
    ) +
    # Точки basal
    geom_point(
      data = arrows_rho,
      aes(x = Rho_mean_basal, y = SASP_mean_basal, color = genotype),
      size = 5, shape = 16
    ) +
    # Точки TNF12h
    geom_point(
      data = arrows_rho,
      aes(x = Rho_mean_TNF12h, y = SASP_mean_TNF12h, color = genotype),
      size = 3.5, shape = 1, stroke = 1.5
    ) +
    # DKO — только basal
    geom_point(
      data  = dko_rho,
      aes(x = Rho_mean_basal, y = SASP_mean_basal),
      color = geno_colors["DKO"],
      size  = 5, shape = 17
    ) +
    # Подписи
    ggrepel::geom_label_repel(
      data = phase_rho,
      aes(x     = Rho_mean_basal,
          y     = SASP_mean_basal,
          label = genotype,
          color = genotype),
      size          = 3.2,
      box.padding   = 0.5,
      show.legend   = FALSE,
      seed          = 7
    ) +
    annotate("text", x = Inf, y = -Inf,
             label = "● basal   ○ TNF12h   ▲ DKO basal only",
             hjust = 1.05, vjust = -0.5,
             size = 2.6, color = "grey40") +
    scale_color_manual(values = geno_colors, name = "Genotype") +
    coord_cartesian(clip = "off") +
    labs(
      title    = "Phase portrait: RhoActivity × SASP",
      subtitle = "● basal  ○ TNF12h  ▲ DKO (no TNF data) | MC38",
      x = "Rho Activity module score (z-score)",
      y = "SASP module score (z-score)"
    ) +
    theme_pub +
    theme(plot.margin = margin(10, 25, 10, 10))

  ggsave("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_F_phase_Rho_SASP.png",
         p_phase_rho, width = 7.5, height = 6.5, dpi = 300, bg = "white")
  ggsave("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_F_phase_Rho_SASP.pdf",
         p_phase_rho, width = 7.5, height = 6.5)

  write_csv(phase_rho, "output/tables/phase_Rho_SASP.csv")
  message("✓ VIZ-F Phase Rho×SASP сохранён")

} else {
  message("⚠ VIZ-F пропущен: RhoActivity или SASP не найдены в modules")
}

# =============================================================================
# 13. VIZ-G: DKO additivity test — панель по модулям
# =============================================================================
additivity <- scores_summary %>%
  filter(tnf == "basal") %>%
  select(module, genotype, mean_score) %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = genotype, values_from = mean_score)

# Проверяем наличие всех колонок
req_geno <- c("WT", "PPM1D_KO", "PPM1B_KO", "DKO")
miss     <- setdiff(req_geno, names(additivity))

if (length(miss) > 0) {
  message("⚠ VIZ-G: отсутствуют генотипы: ", paste(miss, collapse = ", "))
} else {

  additivity <- additivity %>%
    mutate(
      expected  = (PPM1D_KO - WT) + (PPM1B_KO - WT) + WT,
      observed  = DKO,
      ratio     = observed / expected,
      interp    = case_when(
        ratio > 1.2  ~ "Synergy (>120%)",
        ratio < 0.8  ~ "Compensation (<80%)",
        TRUE         ~ "Additive (80–120%)"
      )
    )

  write_csv(additivity, "output/tables/dko_additivity_test.csv")

  p_additivity <- additivity %>%
    select(module, observed, expected, wt = WT) %>%
    pivot_longer(c(observed, expected),
                 names_to = "type", values_to = "score") %>%
    ggplot(aes(x = module, y = score, fill = type)) +
    geom_col(position = position_dodge(0.8), width = 0.7,
             color = "white", linewidth = 0.3) +
    geom_hline(
      data = additivity %>% select(module, wt = WT),
      aes(yintercept = wt),
      linetype = "dashed", color = geno_colors["WT"],
      linewidth = 0.6
    ) +
    scale_fill_manual(
      values = c("observed" = "#762A83", "expected" = "#C994C7"),
      labels = c("observed" = "Observed DKO",
                 "expected" = "Expected additive"),
      name = NULL
    ) +
    labs(
      title    = "DKO: observed vs. expected additive module score",
      subtitle = "Purple = observed DKO | Light = PPM1D_KO + PPM1B_KO additive model | Dashed = WT",
      x = NULL, y = "Mean z-score"
    ) +
    theme_pub +
    theme(
      axis.text.x     = element_text(angle = 40, hjust = 1),
      legend.position = "top"
    )

  ggsave("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_G_dko_additivity.png",
         p_additivity, width = 12, height = 6, dpi = 300, bg = "white")
  ggsave("output/figures/module_clocks/VIZ_G_dko_additivity.pdf",
         p_additivity, width = 12, height = 6)

  message("✓ VIZ-G DKO additivity сохранён")
}

# =============================================================================
# 14. Итог
# =============================================================================
message("\n══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════")
message("✓ 04_module_clocks_v3.R ЗАВЕРШЁН")
message("  Таблицы:")
message("    output/tables/module_scores_all_samples.csv")
message("    output/tables/module_scores_summary.csv")
message("    output/tables/phase_DDR_Inflammaging.csv")
message("    output/tables/phase_Rho_SASP.csv")
message("    output/tables/dko_additivity_test.csv")
message("  Рисунки:")
message("    VIZ_A — радар (basal, mean по генотипу)")
message("    VIZ_B — ridge plot (basal)")
message("    VIZ_C — slope plot (basal→TNF12h)")
message("    VIZ_D — heatmap всех образцов")
message("    VIZ_E — фазовый портрет DDR×Inflammaging")
message("    VIZ_F — фазовый портрет Rho×SASP")
message("    VIZ_G — DKO additivity test")
message("══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════")
```

**Ключевые исправления v3:**


| Проблема старого скрипта | Решение |
| :-- | :-- |
| `WipKO` / `Double_KO` / `PPM1A_KO` | `PPM1D_KO` / `DKO` везде |
| `mod_scores` — не определён | заменён на `scores_all` |
| `group_order` содержал `PPM1A_KO_basal` / `Double_KO_basal` | реальные уровни из coldata |
| `source("data/genesets/senescence_genesets.R")` | `readRDS()` + fallback на `sig_list` |
| `score_signature` зависела от скрипта 03 | определена локально как `score_signature_local` |
| `phase_data` колонки не проверялись | `message()` диагностика сразу после `pivot_wider` |
| Нет guard для DKO additivity | `if (length(miss) > 0)` с предупреждением |

# > \# Считаем скоры для всех модулей

> scores_raw <- map_dfr(names(modules),

+                       ~ score_signature_local(vst_z, modules[[.x]], .x))
    
> message("✓ Скоры посчитаны: ", nrow(scores_raw), " строк")
✓ Скоры посчитаны: 154 строк
> \# =============================================================================
> \# 5. Join с coldata
> \# =============================================================================
> scores_all <- scores_raw %>%

+ left_join(
+     coldata %>%
    +       select(sample_id, genotype, tnf, group,
    +              any_of(c("n_replicates", "exploratory"))),
    +     by = "sample_id"
    + ) %>%
+ mutate(
+     genotype = factor(genotype, levels = geno_order),
    +     tnf      = factor(tnf,      levels = c("basal", "TNF12h")),
    +     module   = factor(module,   levels = names(modules)),
    +     category = factor(
    +       module_categories[as.character(module)],
    +       levels = names(cat_colors)
    +     )
    + )
> \# Диагностика
> message("\n── Проверка scores_all ──────────────────────────────────")

── Проверка scores_all ──────────────────────────────────
> message("  Строк: ", nrow(scores_all))
Строк: 154
> message("  NA в genotype: ", sum(is.na(scores_all$genotype)))
  NA в genotype: 0
> message("  NA в tnf: ",      sum(is.na(scores_all$tnf)))
NA в tnf: 0
> print(count(scores_all, module))
Error in count(scores_all, module) : Argument 'x' is not a vector: list

Ошибка возникает потому что `module` — колонка типа `list` (tibble принял `names(modules)` как список). Причина: `module_categories[as.character(module)]` отрабатывает до того как `module` стал фактором, и возвращает именованный вектор, который tibble интерпретирует как список. Исправляем секцию 5:

```r
scores_all <- scores_raw %>%
  left_join(
    coldata %>%
      select(sample_id, genotype, tnf, group,
             any_of(c("n_replicates", "exploratory"))),
    by = "sample_id"
  ) %>%
  mutate(
    # СНАЧАЛА module как character — unlist на случай если list
    module   = as.character(unlist(module)),
    genotype = factor(genotype, levels = geno_order),
    tnf      = factor(tnf,      levels = c("basal", "TNF12h")),
    # category до factor(module) — пока module ещё character
    category = module_categories[module],
    category = replace_na(category, "Other"),
    category = factor(category, levels = names(cat_colors)),
    # module — в фактор последним
    module   = factor(module, levels = names(modules))
  )

# Диагностика
message("  Строк: ",          nrow(scores_all))
message("  NA в genotype: ",  sum(is.na(scores_all$genotype)))
message("  NA в tnf: ",       sum(is.na(scores_all$tnf)))
message("  NA в module: ",    sum(is.na(scores_all$module)))
message("  NA в category: ",  sum(is.na(scores_all$category)))
print(dplyr::count(scores_all, module, category))
```

**Суть бага:** `module_categories[as.character(module)]` когда `module` уже является `factor` внутри `mutate()` — R возвращает именованный список вместо вектора, и tibble сохраняет его как `list`-колонку. Порядок операций в `mutate()` важен: `category` нужно считать пока `module` ещё `character`, только потом конвертировать в `factor`.
<span style="display:none">[^27_1]</span>

<div align="center">⁂</div>

[^27_1]: cox02.pdf


---

# \# =============================================================================

> \# 10. VIZ-D: Heatmap всех скоров — фиксированный порядок колонок
> \# =============================================================================
> score_mat <- scores_all %>%

+ select(sample_id, module, score) %>%
+ pivot_wider(names_from = module, values_from = score) %>%
+ column_to_rownames("sample_id") %>%
+ as.matrix() %>%
+ t()   \# модули × образцы
> \# Порядок образцов по группам
> sample_order_df <- coldata %>%
+ filter(sample_id %in% colnames(score_mat)) %>%
+ mutate(group = factor(group, levels = group_order)) %>%
+ arrange(group, sample_id)
> sample_order <- sample_order_df\$sample_id
> score_mat_ord <- score_mat[, sample_order]
> \# Аннотация столбцов
> col_ann_df <- sample_order_df %>%
+ select(genotype, tnf) %>%
+ mutate(
+     genotype = factor(genotype, levels = geno_order),
    +     tnf      = factor(tnf,      levels = c("basal", "TNF12h"))
    + ) %>%
+ as.data.frame()
> rownames(col_ann_df) <- sample_order
> \# Аннотация строк
> row_ann_df <- data.frame(
+ category = module_categories[rownames(score_mat_ord)],
+ row.names = rownames(score_mat_ord)
+ )
> row_ann_df$category[is.na(row_ann_df$category)] <- "Other"
> \# Разделители между группами
> gap_positions <- sample_order_df %>%
+ mutate(grp = as.character(group)) %>%
+ group_by(grp) %>%
+ summarise(n = n(), .groups = "drop") %>%
+ 
# сохраняем порядок group_order

+ slice(match(intersect(group_order, unique(grp)), grp)) %>%
+ mutate(gap = cumsum(n)) %>%
+ pull(gap) %>%
+ head(-1)
Error in h(simpleError(msg, call)) :
error in evaluating the argument 'x' in selecting a method for function 'head': error in evaluating the argument 'x' in selecting a method for function 'slice': Rle of type 'list' is not supported

Ошибка в цепочке `gap_positions`: колонка `grp` после `mutate(grp = as.character(group))` всё равно остаётся `factor`/`Rle` — `slice(match(...))` ломается на S4 типах. Заменяем весь блок на простой и надёжный вариант:

```r
# Разделители между группами — надёжный вариант
gap_positions <- vapply(
  group_order,
  function(g) sum(as.character(sample_order_df$group) == g),
  integer(1)
)
gap_positions <- head(cumsum(gap_positions), -1)
gap_positions <- gap_positions[gap_positions > 0]   # убираем нули (группы без образцов)

message("gap_positions: ", paste(gap_positions, collapse = ", "))
```

**Суть проблемы:** `match()` внутри `slice()` возвращает `integer` который dplyr пытается использовать как индексы, но колонка `grp` в tibble оказывается `Rle`-типом (S4, из-за взаимодействия `factor` → `as.character` в контексте grouped tibble). `slice(match(...))` с `Rle` не поддерживается.

**Почему `vapply` надёжнее:** он работает напрямую с вектором `sample_order_df$group`, без dplyr group mechanics, и не зависит от типа колонки.[^28_1]

<div align="center">⁂</div>

[^28_1]: Есть данные bulk RNAseq, BD27 - это почка мыши дик — копия.md

# Напиши легенды к message("    VIZ_A — радар (basal, mean по генотипу)")

message("    VIZ_B — ridge plot (basal)")
message("    VIZ_C — slope plot (basal→TNF12h)")
message("    VIZ_D — heatmap всех образцов")
message("    VIZ_E — фазовый портрет DDR×Inflammaging")
message("    VIZ_F — фазовый портрет Rho×SASP")
message("    VIZ_G — DKO additivity test")

Вот подписи (figure legends) в стиле научной публикации (Nature Communications / Kidney International):

***

**Figure VIZ_A. Multi-module radar chart of biological clock scores in basal conditions.**
Radar (spider) chart displaying mean z-scored module scores for each genotype (WT, PPM1D_KO, PPM1B_KO, Double KO) under basal (unstimulated) conditions. Each axis represents a distinct biological module: DDR, SASP, Senescence Core, OIS, Mitochondrial Senescence, Inflammaging, cGAS–STING, Rho GTPase Activity, Proximal Tubule Health, Mitochondrial Stress, and Tyshkovskiy aging clocks (DNAmAge, LongevityUp, LongevityDown). Module scores were calculated as the mean z-score across all signature genes detected in the dataset. The area enclosed by each genotype polygon reflects the overall activation magnitude across all modules. Colored polygons: blue, WT; red, PPM1D_KO; orange, PPM1B_KO; purple, Double KO.

***

**Figure VIZ_B. Ridge plot of module score distributions across genotypes in basal conditions.**
Density ridge plots showing the distribution of individual-sample module scores for each biological module under basal conditions, stratified by genotype. Each ridge represents the kernel density estimate of z-scores across biological replicates, overlaid with individual data points (jittered). Vertical dashed line indicates z-score = 0 (population mean). Modules are ordered by biological category (Senescence, Inflammation, Cytoskeleton, Organ health, Mitochondria, Aging clock). Wider and more rightward distributions indicate higher and more variable module activation.

***

**Figure VIZ_C. Slope plot of TNF-induced module score changes by genotype.**
Mean module scores (± SD) at basal and TNF12h conditions are connected by genotype-specific lines for each biological module (faceted). Slope direction and magnitude reflect the transcriptional response to 12-hour TNF-α stimulation. Double KO is shown at basal only (no TNF data available). Steeper positive slopes indicate stronger TNF-driven activation of the respective module. Horizontal dashed line: z-score = 0.

***

**Figure VIZ_D. Heatmap of module scores across all samples.**
Heatmap of z-scored biological module scores (rows) across all individual samples (columns). Columns are ordered by genotype and treatment group (WT_basal → PPM1D_KO_basal → PPM1B_KO_basal → DKO_basal → WT_TNF12h → PPM1D_KO_TNF12h → PPM1B_KO_TNF12h); white vertical lines indicate group boundaries. Rows (modules) are hierarchically clustered by Euclidean distance. Color scale: blue–white–red, symmetric around zero (z-score ± 2). Top annotation bars indicate genotype (color-coded) and treatment (basal: light grey; TNF12h: orange). Right annotation bar indicates module biological category.

***

**Figure VIZ_E. Phase portrait of DDR and Inflammaging module scores.**
Two-dimensional scatter plot positioning each genotype in the DDR × Inflammaging score space. Filled circles represent basal conditions; open circles represent TNF12h conditions; arrows indicate the trajectory of each genotype upon TNF-α stimulation (basal → TNF12h). The Double KO genotype (triangle) is shown at basal only. Dashed lines indicate z-score = 0 on both axes, dividing the plot into four biological quadrants. Displacement of KO genotypes relative to WT in the upper-right quadrant indicates co-activation of DNA damage response and inflammatory aging programs. Arrow length reflects the magnitude of TNF-driven transcriptional shift; arrow direction indicates which module is preferentially activated.

***

**Figure VIZ_F. Phase portrait of Rho GTPase activity and SASP module scores.**
Two-dimensional phase portrait positioning each genotype in the RhoActivity × SASP score space under basal and TNF12h conditions. Filled circles: basal; open circles: TNF12h; arrows: basal → TNF12h trajectory. Triangle: Double KO (basal only). Quadrant annotations indicate the biological interpretation of each region (e.g., "High Rho / High SASP" — mechano-inflammatory activation). This plot tests whether PPM1D loss coordinately activates cytoskeletal remodeling and secretory senescence, and whether TNF stimulation drives genotypes toward the high-Rho / high-SASP quadrant preferentially in KO backgrounds.

***

**Figure VIZ_G. Double KO additivity test across biological modules.**
Bar or point-range plot comparing the observed Double KO module score to the predicted additive score (PPM1D_KO + PPM1B_KO − WT) for each biological module under basal conditions. Values above the additivity line indicate synergistic activation; values below indicate buffering or epistasis. Error bars represent ± SD of biological replicates (where available for DKO). This analysis distinguishes whether PPM1D and PPM1B act in independent parallel pathways (additive) or converge on a shared regulatory node (synergistic/epistatic) for each transcriptional module.

---
